Special Article

Chen Kecheng on the Current Disaster Relief Problem 106

China is afflicted by heavenly disaster; calamities strike year after year. First, there was the devastating flood of the 20th year of the Republic, followed by the unprecedented national crisis. Just as the people of the nation were struggling with internal and external troubles, a sudden drought struck, impossible to stop, turning vast stretches of land into red earth, fields cracking, leaving the moribund rural economy to declare its final collapse. According to the previous report of the Relief Committee, this year's drought-stricken provinces number eleven, with the stricken counties reaching 263. In terms of farmland area, even the fertile Jiangsu Province has a staggering 35.75 million mu. Other provinces, uninvestigated areas, and regions affected by floods and insect plagues are beyond count. Given the poverty of our nation's economic foundation and the fragility of its social structure, the Yellow Terrace's melons cannot withstand repeated plucking. Yet, disaster repeatedly strikes, driving us to the brink of ruin. Is Heaven truly abandoning us, or is this a cause for deep sorrow?

The affected area this time is so vast, and the degree of suffering so profound. A picture of disaster victims fleeing, selling wives and children in misery, is beyond our comprehension. It is even more impossible for those in urban comfort and ease to imagine. In the blink of an eye, winter will arrive, and the disaster victims will have no clothes to cover themselves, no food to fill their bellies, howling in the wilderness, shivering and awaiting death. Who does not have parents? Who does not have children? Considering their situation, no one can be unfeeling. Therefore, those who have not suffered should, in good conscience, act with sincerity and provide assistance. Now, each province is discussing winter defense, seeking to protect the people. However, those who commit crimes and threaten winter defense are mostly driven by hunger and cold, unwilling to perish in a ditch. The ancient philosophers had a saying: "With full granaries, people know etiquette and shame." The common people seek only to live. If there is no way to live, they will not hesitate to use any means. It is not their fault that they resort to desperate measures; it is the environment that drives them. Their actions are pitiable, and their situation is understandable. Therefore, if we want to achieve social order and stability and quell banditry, we must first address the problem of comforting the disaster victims. Furthermore, when it comes to plotting resistance against aggression and striving for survival, it is impossible to save the nation without stabilizing the people's lives and strengthening their power. If China is as it is today, with cries of misery everywhere, it will become a breeding ground for bandits and a source of chaos, leaving us unable to focus on domestic issues and without the means to resist foreign aggression. This is a matter of national consciousness that should be addressed urgently and made a priority.

In the matter of disaster relief, the central government has been actively planning, but given the current depletion of the treasury, the enormity of expenses, and the immense need for disaster relief, it relies on the generous assistance of our compatriots. The recent mass donation campaign initiated by Mayor Wu and others in Shanghai is intended to awaken the attention of Shanghai citizens and lead them to open their purses and rescue those in distress. Now that the association has officially begun its work and is meticulously planning various projects, we firmly believe that the results will be remarkable, given Shanghai's past enthusiasm for disaster relief donations, which has been followed by major cities across the country. With the mayor's call to action, we are confident that the results will be impressive. However, as this major fundraising effort begins, we have one more thing to say: we hope that citizens will deeply understand the profound meaning of this initiative by the organizers and donate generously, providing timely assistance. Those who are involved in the process should ensure that the procedures are clearer and the credit is more established. We hear that more than a dozen groups are participating in this fundraising effort, so the procedures for collecting and disbursing funds must be strictly regulated to avoid criticism and ensure that every penny is used effectively, so that the organizers' grand vision is not in vain and the efficiency of disaster relief is enhanced. After mentioning the importance of disaster relief, we wish to express our sincere hope!

Municipal Chamber of Commerce Sends Representatives to Petition for Prompt Change to Brokerage Tax 107

And Requests Suspension of Enforcement Before the Measures Are Announced

After the Municipal Finance Bureau implemented the new brokerage tax regulations, various industry associations believed that they were difficult to implement and had repeatedly submitted petitions through the Chamber of Commerce to the Municipal Government to request a reduction. The details have been recorded in this newspaper. It is now learned that the Municipal Chamber of Commerce has reported that the Finance Bureau, before resolving the disputes over the new brokerage tax regulations, immediately dispatched police to demand payment, causing great panic among the brokerage merchants in various industries. The association has specially sent Pan Xusheng, director of the General Affairs Department, and Xin Dingshan, a representative of the Coal and Charcoal Industry Association, to the Municipal Government at 10:00 AM yesterday to urge the prompt announcement of the revised measures for the brokerage tax and the temporary suspension of enforcement before the measures are announced. The original text is recorded as follows: Submission for Petition. On the first day of this month, we received a letter from the Coal and Charcoal Industry Association stating that, "According to our members Xieji, Wang Changji, Tongyu, and other firms, representatives came to the association to complain, 'To whom it may concern: Our members Xieji, Wang Changji, Tongyu, and other firms, representatives came to the association to complain that the Municipal Public Security Bureau has dispatched police to our firms to order us to fill out the application forms and guarantee forms newly issued by the Finance Bureau within three days and apply for new licenses from the South Municipal Taxation Office ourselves. We have been applying for new licenses from the brokerage tax collection office through your association without interruption or concealment since our firms were established. This year, due to the new regulations issued by the Municipal Finance Bureau, which are difficult to implement, and the taxation office's refusal to grant the issuance of new licenses according to past practice, we have been unable to comply. At the same time, your association contacted various brokerage industry associations to request the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to argue on the basis of reason and sent representatives to the Municipal Government to petition. Now, the Finance Bureau is dispatching police to demand payment without waiting for the Municipal Government to resolve the matter. Such a situation is making it impossible for merchants to comply. Therefore, we urge your association to promptly remedy the situation to reassure the business community.' This association has repeatedly requested your association to find a way to provide relief since the Municipal Finance Bureau issued the new regulations, and sent representatives to the Municipal Government to petition and submitted an outline for your association to forward. Now that the Finance Bureau is dispatching police to demand payment while the Municipal Government is carefully considering the matter and merchants are waiting for a solution, such a situation seems like oppression. We are sending a letter and asking Xin Dingsan to go to your association to explain everything. We respectfully request that you send representatives to the Municipal Government to argue again that this case should not be implemented until it is resolved and order the Public Security Bureau to suspend enforcement to avoid causing panic among merchants and creating major disputes." The association has received letters from various industries related to the brokerage tax, stating that the new regulations restrict brokerage commissions and are very different from the actual business situation. If implemented, no brokerage firm can survive. We requested that you forward it to the Municipal Government for review and revision on October 13th, detailing the reasons. Afterwards, various industries sent explanations, which were sent to the Secretariat of the Municipal Government for review. The difficulties of various industries and the necessity of revising the new regulations must be clear. On November 3rd, various industries urged us to submit another petition to your government, requesting that you inform the Finance Bureau to temporarily suspend the implementation of the new regulations before they are revised, and to temporarily suspend the renewal of expired brokerage licenses. It has been more than a month, and we have not received a response. However, the Finance Bureau has suddenly rigorously implemented the new regulations and dispatched police to demand payment, ignoring the previous requests of the merchants. Various industries are extremely worried and unable to remain silent. They have submitted another petition to Pan Xusheng, director of the General Affairs Department, to present the previous situation to your government, requesting that you promptly announce the revised measures for the brokerage tax and temporarily suspend the renewal of expired licenses until the new measures are announced, in order to appease the hopes of the merchants. It is for the public benefit. We respectfully submit this to the Shanghai Municipal Government.

Stores in the First Special District, in order to relieve the disaster victims in Zhejiang, have established a recruitment team in the First Special District. Shanghai County Miscellaneous Taxes Determined to Abolish Collection 109

Seven Types Collected, Three Types Abolished

The original local miscellaneous taxes in various districts of Shanghai County were previously ordered by the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Finance to be reorganized and collected uniformly by the county. The county then ordered the various district offices to investigate, list, and report to the county for forwarding. The county government has now received instructions from the Department of Finance after reviewing the various miscellaneous taxes in the county and has instructed to follow the instructions to abolish the collection separately. Therefore, the county government announced it yesterday for general knowledge. The items to be collected are: Education ship donation in the first district, teahouse education donation, advertising donation, housing donation and teahouse donation in each district, education donation in deed tax, household registration donation in deed tax, education donation in deed tax. The items to be abolished are: Voluntary donation of the security corps in the first district, road and lamp donation in each district, and fishing household tax in the fourth district.

the form of British Garden Cities, while incorporating the meaning of Japanese New Villages, to improve Chinese social life. It is not only to solve the housing problem for society. enable the propertyless to own property. It strives to enable households to turn consumption into growth, obtain comfortable housing, a beautiful environment, realize a happy life, and establish a healthy family. to complete the ideal New Village, so the solicitation for signing up will end at the end of this year. Robbery at Tianbaocheng Gold Shop Sentenced 118

Zao Zhaoyu, a native of Ningbo, sneaked into Tianbaocheng Gold Shop at 615 East Seward Road at 2:50 PM on the 23rd of last month. Under the pretext of exchanging gold rings, he forcibly took them and escaped. Shi Yonglun, a shop assistant, jumped out of the counter and chased him frantically, shouting "Catch the thief!" He was intercepted by Hua Detective You Youming, who brought him and the stolen goods to the Huishan Police Station, and then escorted him to the First Special District Court for investigation. Yesterday, Judge Xiao Xiexuan came to the court for a further hearing. Li Zhishan, a lawyer from the Public Works Department, stated that no other cases had been found during the period of adjournment. He requested that the defendant's confession be investigated. The defendant confessed that he had resorted to this scheme because he was poor and unable to make a living. He pleaded for leniency. Judge Xiao sentenced Zao Zhaoyu to two months' imprisonment and ordered that the stolen goods be returned to their original owner.

Two Wives of Cheng Zhong'an Sue for Status, Judgment Rendered 119

Cheng Jiang is dissatisfied and must appeal

Cheng Zhong'an, a native of Sichuan, was a sundry goods broker who traveled between Shanghai, Beiping, and other places. He was skilled in business and accumulated a considerable fortune. In March of this year, Cheng Zhong'an went to Beiping to do business and unfortunately died of illness. When the bad news came, Jiang Yueying (i.e., Cheng Jiang), a woman from Songjiang, and Li Abao (i.e., Cheng Li), a local woman, filed lawsuits in the local court one after another over the issue of status, demanding to be recognized as Cheng Zhong'an's wife. They also slandered each other, accusing the other party of being a concubine, while claiming to be Cheng Zhong'an's formal wife. Because the case was unusually complicated, the court spared no effort to seek details, repeatedly ordering the matchmakers and witnesses presented by both sides to appear in court to describe the past events and the marriage situation. It is learned that this case has been debated to a conclusion and the judgment has been announced the day before yesterday: (Main Text) Cheng Jiang's lawsuit is dismissed; Cheng Li is recognized as the wife of the deceased Cheng Zhong'an. The verdicts have already been served separately. It is heard that Cheng Jiang is dissatisfied with the verdict and will appeal according to law.

Tong Gaofeng Commits Suicide in Hotel 120

Tong Gaofeng, a native of Shaoxing, 49 years old this year, was engaged in the business of foreign socks in Shanghai. Recently, for some unknown reason, he suddenly had a pessimistic idea. One night, he bought raw opium and went to the Xinquanxing Inn at 398 Minquan Road in the French Concession, booking room number three to stay overnight. He committed suicide by swallowing poison that night. At 9 AM yesterday morning, Zhou Xingyu, a waiter, urged him to get up but received no response. When he entered the room to check, he saw that Tong's face was pale and he could not open his mouth. Knowing that he had committed suicide by taking poison, he immediately reported it to the Innkeepers' Association, which sent someone to check and then reported it to the French Concession Police. A detective was dispatched to investigate. At noon, he was taken to Renji Hospital, but he had been poisoned too deeply and could not be saved. He died at 1:30 PM. The hospital notified the police, who transported the body to the Tongren Funeral Parlor for an autopsy. Since there was no household registration, the Special Second Court will be requested to send someone to examine the body this morning.

Peanuts and Other Items Exempt from Transit Tax for Two Years 121

Jianghai Customs Ordered to Issue Public Notice for General Knowledge

Starting from November 29th of this year

Tang Haian, the Superintendent of Jianghai Customs, and Burkhardt, the Customs Commissioner, issued Joint Public Notice No. 1405 yesterday regarding the exemption of transit tax for peanuts, peanut kernels, peanut oil, and other items for two years: "In accordance with Instruction No. 9877 from the Ministry of Finance, it has been approved that peanuts, peanut kernels, and peanut oil transported from Shanghai to various ports in the country shall be exempt from transit tax for two years." This should be followed. The transit tax on the aforementioned goods will be exempted for two years starting from November 29th of this year. This is hereby announced to all merchants for their information.

The Improved Chinese Bookkeeping Achievement Exhibition was held yesterday, the second day. Since it was a Sunday and there were celebrity lectures, the number of attendees viewing the displays and listening to the lectures was even greater than on the first day. Many schools and organizations also participated. The City Chamber of Commerce's assembly hall and the display rooms on the third floor were overcrowded, and many people had to leave. Throughout the day, over 8,000 people viewed the displays and listened to the lectures. At 10 AM, the lecture meeting began. First, Mr. Wang Yansong delivered the opening remarks, followed by Mr. Xu Yongzuo's report on the process and opinions regarding the improvement of Chinese bookkeeping. The celebrities who gave lectures included prominent figures in the business community, such as Lin Kanghou, Wang Xiaolai, Qin Runqing, and Luo Qinghua, as well as Lin Jinyu, the Director of the Nanjing Audit Department. Other notable figures, such as Yu Zuoting, the Chairman of the Chamber of Commerce, Xu Jipin, a standing committee member, Wen Yiyou, the Director of the Accounting Bureau of the National Government's Accounting Office, as well as Pan Yangyao, Sheng Zhuo'er, Ji Jiannan, and Tao Leqin, were also prepared to give lectures, but were unable to do so due to the lateness of the hour. The details are as follows:

Meeting Order 1. Ringing the bell to open the meeting; 2. All stand at attention and pay the highest respect to the Party and National Flags and the Portrait of the Premier; 3. Reverently read the Premier's Will; 4. Mr. Wang Yansong delivers the opening remarks; 5. Mr. Xu Yongzuo reports on the process of improving Chinese bookkeeping; 6. Celebrity lectures; 7. Ringing the bell to adjourn the meeting.

Opening Remarks First, Mr. Wang Yansong delivered the opening remarks, stating briefly that accounting is closely related to industry and commerce, and the City Chamber of Commerce is responsible for promoting industry and commerce. It has always attached importance to various matters related to industrial and commercial management, and accounting is one aspect of it. It is well known that bookkeeping in our country is poor, and the City Chamber of Commerce deeply felt the need to improve it. Accountant Xu Yongzuo also felt the same way, so he jointly organized an improved Chinese bookkeeping training course this year. The first cohort has now graduated, and they should make a significant contribution to the industrial and commercial community. He hopes that the graduates will continue to work hard in the future to promote and develop the improved Chinese bookkeeping method, and use their learning to engage in the actual work of improvement, so that the general industrial and commercial community can benefit from it. Bookkeeping in our country has a long history, and it has many advantages, but unfortunately, it has always been thought of as something that ordinary people could learn, leading to disorder and uncertainty, which greatly hinders industrial and commercial management. Since Western bookkeeping was introduced to China, although it seems to be orderly, the principles are complex and the costs are high, and the bookkeeping talent cannot be achieved in a short-term training program. It is not easy to promote to the general bookkeeping community, so the Chinese and Western methods have never been communicated. Those who use the Chinese method do not know the scientific methods of the Western method, and those who use the Western method do not understand the habits of the Chinese method. We want to find a moderate and easy method, and we can only adopt the improved Chinese bookkeeping method. We can only promote the improved Chinese bookkeeping method. The students of the training course should be aware of the importance of their mission. Please, all of you celebrities present, give us more advice to supplement what the training has not covered.

Report on the Process Next, Accountant Xu Yongzuo reported, stating briefly that since the introduction of Western bookkeeping to China, Chinese bookkeeping has been despised by people for a long time. However, for the past three or four decades, except for banks, railways, and new enterprises, Chinese bookkeeping has been as prevalent as ever, and its simplicity and incompleteness have remained the same. Remaining in this state for a long time has a huge impact on the national economy and the people's livelihood. Although I am trained in Western bookkeeping, in the past ten years, I have felt that Western bookkeeping is not easy to promote, and Chinese bookkeeping is difficult to abandon. I advocate guiding the situation and improving Chinese bookkeeping. Since the publication of the improved Chinese bookkeeping plan and special book last winter, it has aroused the attention of the whole country. Last winter, we held an exhibition and lecture meeting at the City Chamber of Commerce, and at that time, many listeners requested to run a training course, but it did not happen due to being busy. Since the beginning of this year, more and more people have adopted the improved Chinese bookkeeping method, and more and more people have requested to run a training course. Therefore, I discussed the charter with Mr. Yan, the Principal of the Commercial School of the City Chamber of Commerce, and started this subject. Since publishing the announcement in the newspaper in late July, more than 800 people have come to study in less than ten days. Because the classroom could no longer accommodate them, we had to stop enrolling early and started school on August 1st. We taught for one hour a day, and it was completed in two months. Although the time was short, the students were able to study hard, so the results were still good. I would also like to ask all of you present to give us more guidance.

Lin Kanghou's Speech Briefly stated that I am a very old-fashioned person, and I have not studied either Chinese bookkeeping or Western bookkeeping. However, I feel that the Chinese and Western methods each have their own strengths and weaknesses, and each has its own applicable place. The adoption should be based on one's own circumstances, and it is not necessary to adopt the Western method to be considered new. It is also not necessary to think that you have completely learned something. Accountant Xu Yongzuo's improved Chinese bookkeeping extracts the scientific spirit of the Western method and integrates it, and uses the inherent habits of the Chinese method and improves them. Integration and understanding is easy to implement. Although I am an old-fashioned person, I also feel that it is very perfect and quite commendable. Some people measure the merits of Chinese and Western methods by the distinction between horizontal and vertical formats. I think it is unnecessary, because horizontal and vertical formats have their own considerable value in themselves. However, we have always read books in a vertical format and written in a vertical format, so we feel that the vertical format of Chinese bookkeeping is more practical. Now that we are promoting a new life, everyone is paying attention to it. In fact, the goal of the new life is to restore the old morality. For Western bookkeepers, it is not impossible to view talking about improving Chinese bookkeeping in this way. Others may judge the application of Chinese and Western methods by the difference between new and old businesses. I think the views should be far-reaching. How broad is the situation in China that is suitable for the Chinese method? It is not possible to limit it to several urban foreign-style organizations. Accountant Xu is an old friend of mine. Although I do not understand the mysteries of bookkeeping, I feel that his improved Chinese bookkeeping is both understandable and feasible. Please, everyone, jointly promote it.

Wang Xiaolai's Speech Briefly stated that we should reform everything that we feel is not applicable or does not meet the needs of the times. The so-called reformers are not intended to stick to the old methods, nor are they intended to imitate foreign countries. For example, if bookkeeping continues to use the inherent methods without change, it is conservatism. If it completely adopts Western methods, it is imitation. Neither is right. We must retain the strengths of the inherent methods and remove the shortcomings in order to be called reform. However, there is a distinction between improving and worsening reform. It must be changed for the better in order to be practical. If it is changed for the worse, it is better not to change it. Accountant Xu Yongzuo's improved Chinese bookkeeping is a change for the better. We only ask whether the reform is appropriate, and we can ignore how it is done.

Lin Jinyu's Speech Briefly stated that I have several thoughts on the improved Chinese bookkeeping method: 1. The general public regards accounting as a minor skill. Scholars and officials are ashamed to talk about goods and profits. The economic difficulties of China's public and private sectors are not unrelated to this. Since I went abroad to study until now, I have never left the accounting field. I have found that the importance of accounting is beyond what the general public imagines. However, I have not seen many people in the country who can deeply pay attention to this and preside over the meeting to seek universal improvement. Now I am fortunate that Accountant Xu is promoting the reform of our country's inherent Chinese bookkeeping method. How happy I am to come all the way from Nanjing to participate in this grand event. 2. Theory and practice cannot be neglected. Chinese and Western bookkeeping methods each have their own strengths in theory, but in practice, we should consider which one to adopt. As far as the present is concerned, the use of the improved Chinese bookkeeping method should be more common in various parts of China. This cannot be denied. Some say that the development of industry comes from need, and if Western bookkeeping is popular, China will be able to produce its own pens, ink, paper, and Zhangzi. There is a reasonable point in this statement, but it cannot be said for the time being. In my opinion, the principle is that science is suitable for the times. In the future, horizontal accounts can be improved with the Chinese bookkeeping method, and there is a possibility of gradually becoming horizontal. I saw a lot of things on display at the exhibition. Among the accounts, there is a horizontal daily nuclear table. Is this the beginning? Based on these two thoughts, I feel that when talking about improving Chinese bookkeeping, we should take into account all the problems. It would be more appropriate to name it improving Chinese Bookkeeping.

Qin Runqing's Speech Briefly stated that merchants, whether large or small, have their own books and records. The profits and losses of the business and the verification of debts depend on the accounts. The accounts of our merchants in various industries are different, lack a system, follow the old customs, and are unwilling to change. Although detailed notes are rarely clear, there are still many shortcomings in this. Recently, the European wind has been blowing eastward, and the Western method is popular. Although the bookkeeping continuation is complicated, the records are more detailed than the Chinese method. Now Accountant Xu has initiated the improvement of Chinese bookkeeping and set up a school to teach. The scholars from all over the country are very enthusiastic, which shows the importance of this matter. Moreover, the Chinese bookkeeping method has been simplified, summarized, and improved by Accountant Xu, and has become a model bookkeeping method with clear items and practical use. In the future, if it can be gradually promoted throughout the country and adopted uniformly, it will be a great celebration for the industrial and commercial circles of our country.

Luo Qinghua's Speech Briefly stated that bookkeeping is a kind of social science, and it should be rationalized. The so-called rationalization is to fully exert its "efficiency." The so-called "efficiency" includes three major elements: 1. Accuracy, 2. Simplicity, and 3. Savings. Now, let's talk about the ability of the Chinese and Western bookkeeping methods to meet the conditions of "efficiency." The simplicity and obviousness of Chinese bookkeeping and the saving of expenses are indeed beyond the reach of Western bookkeeping. However, its shortcomings are that the accounts have no fixed format, the accounts have no fixed classification, and the bookkeeping has no fixed rules. In short, it does not meet the principle of accuracy. Western bookkeeping is accurate, but simplicity and saving are not necessary. Therefore, speaking of improving bookkeeping, it is better to take the strengths of the Western method and make up for the shortcomings of the Chinese method. Accountant Xu's improved Chinese bookkeeping is able to meet this principle. All of our Chinese people should unanimously approve and cooperate to promote it. Finally, there is also a report, that is, I recently participated in the meeting of the Legislative Yuan and discussed the Commercial Registration Law. In view of the fact that China's bookkeeping law has not yet been perfected, and the Western bookkeeping law cannot be practical, I advocated that the improved Chinese bookkeeping method should be incorporated into the code after it has been effectively promoted. It can be seen that the improved Chinese bookkeeping method is not only valued by the business community, but also known by the government.

The Amateur National Products Promotion Group Hosted the Press Yesterday 126

Organization Divided into Three Departments: Promotion, Sales, and Entertainment

(Central News Agency) A group of enthusiastic patriotic young people in this city, in order to promote domestic products, specially initiated the organization of the Amateur National Products Promotion Group. The initiators of the group specially hosted the press at Guanshengyuan on the Great Eastern Road at 2 p.m. yesterday. Dozens of reporters from various newspapers attended.

Purpose: First, Li Manyun, one of the founders of the group, reported on the preparation process and organizational details, stating that the group was formed in view of the recent influx of foreign goods into the market and the daily decline of domestic products, resulting in a severe loss of rights and profits. The outflow of wealth is deeply regrettable. The way to remedy this is to improve domestic products, expand promotion, and create a widespread and deep impression of domestic products among the people, so that domestic products can flourish. However, many young people admire foreign things and willingly become salesmen for foreign goods. Even those who serve in the domestic products industry spend their leisure time in dance halls or pursuing music and entertainment, squandering their useful energy in a world of pleasure, and their ambitions are worn down, which is truly heartbreaking. This is why we use our spare time to organize the Amateur Performance Troupe. Although the group has only been initiated for a short time, many ambitious young people have come to participate upon hearing the news, which shows that the people are not dead and the country has great potential. Currently, in addition to using No. 407, Central China Building as the group's address, the first preparatory meeting was held the day before yesterday to discuss the matters to be carried out. At the same time, we will submit the application to the city's party and government agencies for filing, and separately solicit members, in order to promote domestic products and achieve the goal of saving the country with domestic goods. Once the group is fully prepared and formally established, it will use the spare time of each member to carry out the work, such as (1) Promotion Department: (A) Written promotion, the group will compile and print publications to extensively promote pure domestic products. (B) Entertainment promotion, compiling plays that are both cautionary and contain elements of domestic products, and performing in various local and foreign locations during the members' spare time. (C) Lectures, assigning members to give lectures on domestic products in various places. (2) Sales Department: The group will act as an agent for the sale of pure domestic products from manufacturers. (3) Entertainment Department: Providing various legitimate entertainment activities to help the members' interests. He continued that the group is in its early stages of establishment, and everything needs to be done. He hopes that scholars and talents from all walks of life at home and abroad will not hesitate to offer guidance.

Declaration: The Amateur National Products Promotion Group declared, "To revive the nation, the first priority is to revitalize industry, and to recover rights and interests, the only way is to stop the outflow of wealth." Therefore, since the national crisis, the call for promoting domestic products has been loud and the theory of revitalizing industry has been widely advocated. This is because people with insight are trying to save themselves. However, when we examine the results, the dimness of domestic products remains, and the rampantness of foreign goods is even more severe, which makes people shake their heads and sigh. The reason for this is that Chinese people are often superficial and engage in empty talk, with many speaking loudly but few determined to put things into practice. This is one reason. Secondly, the domestic products movement has failed to patiently and earnestly persuade people, leaving them with a deep and indelible impression and arousing the concept of loving and using domestic products. As a result, although the domestic products movement is like bamboo shoots after rain, it has failed to achieve practical results. Is this just a coincidence? Promoting domestic products must involve deep and insightful lectures to awaken our compatriots from their illusions, and cautionary performances to enlighten the people, so as to arouse their enthusiasm for purchasing domestic products and strengthen their patriotic spirit, thereby achieving the grand goal of developing domestic products and the purpose of promoting the sales of domestic products. Therefore, promoting domestic products must begin with performances. We are not talented, but we believe that every citizen is responsible for the rise and fall of the country. How can we sit idly by? Therefore, we dare not overestimate our abilities and have organized the Amateur National Products Performance Troupe to promote domestic products in our spare time, fulfilling the national duty of citizens and seeking the development of industry. We hope that leaders of industry at home and abroad will not hesitate to offer guidance and correct our shortcomings. This is our declaration."

The Greater Shanghai Consumer Cooperative Actively Expands Its Business 128

Welcome New Members to Join

The Greater Shanghai Consumer Cooperative at No. 434 Pubai Road, French Concession, is organized by leaders from various sectors of the Party, government, business, and academia in this city, and aims to promote cooperative enterprises. Therefore, it fully adopts the Rochdale Principles. Since its establishment in January last year, the first settlement resulted in a surplus. However, the cooperative is different from ordinary stores. The profit distribution method is based on the amount of consumption. Therefore, each member enthusiastically purchases from the cooperative, so that rights and interests are not lost. It is now heard that the cooperative is seeking to actively expand its operations and is continuing to solicit new members. Its business scope is temporarily based on daily necessities, such as rice, coal, firewood, charcoal, salt, soy sauce, leather shoes, silver shields, gifts, etc., which are all complete and the prices are lower than the market. The cooperative serves the society and its members. Once a member needs something and notifies them by phone, it will be delivered immediately without additional delivery charges. Detailed rules are printed and available upon request.

Fifty-Eight Gamblers Arrested from Two Gambling Dens in Jiangwan and Nanshi 129

A Large Number of Gambling Tools and Gambling Funds Seized

All Handed Over to the General Bureau for Legal Action

Lu Ying, the captain of the detective team of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, learned that Hou Fusheng, a local from Houqiaobian, Gaojing Temple, Jiangwan Town, had set up a Fuxin Tea Garden and prepared a large number of gambling tools, gathering ignorant people from nearby to gamble day and night, with huge gains and losses. Hou Fusheng profited from it. He ordered detectives Chen Caifu and Dong Wenrui to lead detectives and officers from the Jiangwan Police Station, all in disguise, to secretly go to the tea shop at about 1 a.m. yesterday, pretending to be gamblers and mixing into the gambling venue. While the gamblers were in high spirits, the detectives and officers arrested them. The gamblers tried to jump out of windows and climb over the roof to escape. The order was chaotic for a while. As a result, in addition to arresting the gambling boss Hou Fusheng, 39 gamblers, including Tao Rongsheng, Shen Xijin, Wang Kelang, Li Zuzu, Wang Linsheng, Lu Juxiang, Shen Liansheng, Shen Xiaomao, Wang Yanliang, Tan Tao, Qin Jinshu, Xu Fubao, Gao Yongfa, Lu Taotao, Zhang Lingen, Zhou Miaoxing, Xi Yansheng, Zhang Hongsheng, Meng Yongxiang, Wang Guitang, Gu Shengxiang, Cao Maofu, Yang Caisheng, Ma Songgen, Jiang Fufu, Wang Xiangxiang, Tao Jinfu, etc., were caught on the spot, and gambling tools such as four sets of mahjong tiles, two sets of paper flower cards, and two sets of Pai Gow tiles, and gambling funds of 31 yuan and 44 cents in small change were seized. The team took the suspects to the bureau yesterday morning. The suspects were all vague in their words and were handed over to the Third Section of the General Bureau for handling according to law. In addition, the gambling dens with a cut in No. 6, Lane 193, Liyuan Road, Nanshi, were also investigated by Li, the director of the Ximen Branch of the Municipal Public Security Bureau. He immediately dispatched Chen Shengtiao, a patrol officer from the Liyuan Road Police Substation under his jurisdiction, to secretly go to the address at about 11 p.m. the night before. He arrested the gambling boss Luo Xiaomao and 19 gamblers, including Chen Xiaosan, Xi Xiaomao, Wang Ligen, Chen Dalang, Luo Bingsheng, Qian Linsheng, Xia Chunchun, Yu Heshang, Sun Zhangtao, Lu Youlin, etc. Gambling tools such as playing cards and dice were seized on the spot and taken to the bureau. Yesterday morning, bureau member Lin Qishan summoned the case and interrogated the suspects. They all admitted to gambling. They were handed over to the General Bureau in the afternoon for handling according to law.

Jiang Youqing Was Stabbed in a Friend's House for Speaking Up 130

A Knife from a Beef Stall Was Used as a Murder Weapon

Four Men Fled After Committing the Crime

Jiang Youqing, 35 years old, from Shaoxing, is in the soy sauce business and lives at No. 22 Hongfuli, Xinzha Road. At about 6:50 p.m. yesterday, Jiang had a friend from his hometown come to Shanghai. He was also acquainted with a person nicknamed Xiaomao who lived at No. 10 Hongjili, Soy Sauce Lane, Xinzha Road. After having dinner at Jiang's place, they went together to Xiaomao's house in Hongjili. However, Xiaomao had already gone out and only his wife was at home. At the same time, four other men were sitting in the living room, threatening Xiaomao's wife to collect debts, with a menacing manner. When Jiang Youqing saw that Xiaomao himself was not there, he felt that they should not be threatening his family and spoke up for them, arguing with the debt collectors. They disagreed with each other and started arguing. Unexpectedly, the four men ran to the beef stall at the entrance of the lane, grabbed a beef knife, and stabbed Jiang in the shoulder and back before fleeing. Jiang was seriously injured and unable to chase them, so they escaped. He immediately reported to the police station and had them taken to the hospital for treatment. He also tracked down the murderers.

Residents of Chenxing Lane on Yangshupu Road, Forced to Demolish Mezzanines by the Municipal Council, Appeal for Assistance 133

There are 300 houses in Chenxing Lane on Parker Road in this city, most of which are single-family houses. The residents are all poor people. Due to the high rent, and according to the common practice in Shanghai, they all built awnings and mezzanine floors in the houses. This was discovered by the Engineering Department of the Municipal Council, which first ordered the awnings to be removed. Those who did not have time to remove them were all smashed. The day before yesterday, they ordered the removal of the mezzanine floors, which caused great panic among the residents. They convened a meeting at 2 p.m. yesterday to discuss countermeasures. They decided to send representatives to petition the Municipal Council first. If it is ineffective, all the residents, men, women, old and young, will petition the Municipal Council in teams until the goal is achieved. At the same time, they will submit petitions to the Shanghai Municipal Party Department, the Shanghai Municipal Social Affairs Bureau, the Chinese Ratepayers' Association of the Public Concession, and the Shanghai First Special Zone Citizens' Union, requesting them to uphold justice and provide assistance. The petition to each agency is as follows: "Petition for the Public Concession Municipal Council to impose oppression and discriminate against residents, requesting justice and assistance. We, the tenants of No. 253 Lane, Parker Road, Shanghai (Chenxing Lane), are all brokers. In recent years, the market has been bleak and all industries have been depressed. Life is difficult and it is difficult to make ends meet. The rent for single-family, multi-story houses in this lane is as high as 50 yuan per month, not including the house tax and electricity bill. We, the tenants, cannot afford it, so we also follow the common practice in Shanghai and build awnings and mezzanine floors in the houses to supplement our income. The houses in this lane were completed in September of this year, and the tenants moved in and renovated the houses three months ago, and there was no other reason. Unexpectedly, in October, the Public Concession Municipal Council suddenly sent letters to each tenant, ordering them to remove the awnings within seven days. Some tenants did not have time to remove them due to various reasons. The bureau sent armed patrolmen to lead the workers, who were like wolves and tigers, and smashed and beat them indiscriminately. At that time, all the people in the lane were crying and shouting, and the state was uneasy. On the 28th of last month, the bureau took a step forward and sent letters to each tenant, ordering them to remove the mezzanine floors within seven days. The tenants felt that they had already lost a lot of awnings, and they could not bear to remove the mezzanine floors again. The tenants of this lane sent representatives to the bureau with a document to petition for exemption from removal. The officials from the Engineering Department of the bureau met with them and asked them again and again. They refused to allow it, citing fire hazards. We have found that awnings and mezzanine floors are common decorations in Shanghai and can be seen everywhere. We have never heard of any ban, but we are the only ones being serious about in this lane. Residents are also residents within the boundary. Why are we the only ones being discriminated against? Moreover, the lane has been completed for three months, and tenants have moved in and renovated the houses one after another. The bureau did not disclose any announcements in advance, nor did it stop them halfway. When the houses were completed, they began to ban them. This is simply teasing the residents and arbitrarily imposing oppression. Even if the bureau is learning from the past and planning for the future and will completely remove the awnings and mezzanine floors in Shanghai to prevent fire hazards, then why not publish an announcement in advance and suddenly start from this lane? Most of the tenants in this lane are poor people. To rent these houses and build awnings and mezzanine floors, they have spent hundreds of yuan, many of which are from loans and mortgages. If they are really removed, it is equivalent to bankruptcy, and there will be unimaginable tragic facts. It will also cause great panic throughout Shanghai. Now, the tenants in this lane have held a meeting to discuss and decided to be willing to understand the bureau's intention to prevent fire hazards. The awnings will be re-built according to the license, and the mezzanine floors will not be allowed to be inhabited. We have always admired your departments (bureaus) (associations) for upholding justice and relieving the suffering of the people. We hereby submit a petition to your departments (bureaus) (associations) for review and approval. We humbly ask you to consider the small people and the oppression they have suffered, and that there is no way to appeal. Please grant us assistance and forward a letter to the bureau, allowing the awnings to be re-built according to the license and the mezzanine floors to be used only for storing items and not for living in, in order to prevent fire hazards and relieve the difficulties of the people. This would be a great virtue."

Tenants of Qinyuli, Yangshupu Road, Who Were Cut Off from Water, Ask the City Federation for Relief 135

The Association Sent a Relief Section to Mediate

The owner of Qinyuli on Yangshupu Road in this city, Qinyu Company, cut off the water supply to coerce tenants to increase water fees. The tenants petitioned the Social Affairs Bureau to investigate and order the restoration of the water supply to maintain drinking water. Yesterday, they specially submitted a petition to the Citizens' Union of the First Special Zone, requesting relief. The petition stated that the houses of Qinyuli on Yangshupu Road belong to the owner Li Xueqin and have been leased for five or six years. In the 19th year of the Republic of China, the rent was increased by one yuan, including the water fee. The house ticket also clearly stated that the water in the lane was supplied by the owner. Recently, the owner suddenly used the name of disguised rent increase and forcibly collected a water fee of two yuan per household. Without the consent of the tenants, the owner cut off the water supply to coerce the tenants and demolished the water pipes in the entire lane, cutting off the drinking water of thousands of people and ordering them to move out. The tenants have been oppressed and more than a dozen households have gone bankrupt. The losses suffered are countless. They have to ask your association for relief as soon as possible to save the endangered tenants. Moreover, urban tap water is a necessity for human life. The owner must know that he is only interested in profit and does not care about life. He acts arbitrarily and requests you to send someone to mediate. After learning the situation, the association immediately sent the investigation section to mediate and asked the owner to open the water supply immediately to protect the people's lives and ensure social stability. The two sides are currently in consultation and the water supply will be taken over and opened soon.

High Court Branch Secretary Accused of Embezzlement; Court Grants Non-Prosecution 136

Various documents do not contain any mention of interest coupons.

The court cannot provide evidence unfavorable to the defendant.

Wang Jusheng of Zida Lumber Firm and Wang Xiankang, owner of Changtai Construction Factory, had a dispute over payment for goods at the end of last year. Bian Jialu, a lawyer, represented them and filed a lawsuit in the Second Special District Court's Criminal Division, accusing Wang of issuing a check for 12,000 yuan, along with a civil suit. In January of this year, Jusheng again petitioned the court, requesting a preliminary injunction to seize 13,000 yuan of Wang Xiankang's uncollected construction funds at Dasha Commercial Bank. After the execution court judge approved the injunction, Jusheng was ordered to provide a guarantee. Jusheng complied and submitted twelve long-term financial government bonds of the 17th year of the Republic of China from the Ministry of Finance, each with a face value of 1,000 yuan, totaling 12,000 yuan, to his lawyer, Bian, who submitted them to the court on the 22nd of the same month. Subsequently, the preliminary injunction was implemented. The execution office received the government bonds and transferred them to the accounting department of the High Court Branch for safekeeping. In September, Jusheng and Wang reached an out-of-court settlement, and Jusheng petitioned the court to lift the preliminary injunction and retrieve the

government bonds provided as security. The court approved the request and issued a retrieval order on October 1st, instructing Jusheng to present it to the accounting department of the High Court Branch to collect the government bonds. That afternoon, Jusheng specifically went to the accounting department of the High Court Branch on West Ash Road to collect the financial government bonds. He discovered that twelve interest coupons dated September 30th, totaling 150 yuan, had been clipped off the bonds. He immediately protested. Jusheng wanted to retrieve the original receipt, but the accounting department refused, stating that it had already been registered and canceled. With no resolution, Jusheng had to take back the bonds. However, since the original petition had clearly stated that the bonds included interest coupons dated September 30th, he felt aggrieved by their sudden disappearance. Therefore, he filed a complaint with the Second Special District Court's prosecutor's office, accusing the duty secretary of the High Court Branch's accounting department's fee collection office of

dereliction of duty and embezzlement, requesting investigation. Prosecutor Wang Ren summoned Li Shu (41 years old, from Xiushan, Sichuan), the secretary in charge of the government bonds in the accounting department of the High Court Branch; Feng Bangyan, secretary of the Third Special District Court's dispatch office; Wang Hui and Liu Gui (Liu has since resigned), secretaries of the execution office; and the duty secretary of the fee collection office; as well as the plaintiff Qu Jisheng, witness Song Benren, and Bian Jialu, the lawyer who originally handled Qu's case, to open a court investigation. The details of the case have been reported in previous news. After several thorough investigations by Prosecutor Wang, including inquiries with various banks in central China that handled the bond interest payments and the National Debt Fund Management Committee, it was determined that the interest had not yet been claimed. The investigation concluded that the evidence presented by the plaintiff was insufficient to prove the defendant's

illegal behavior. Therefore, a decision was made to not prosecute the case. The non-prosecution decision has now been delivered. The non-prosecution decision is transcribed below: Non-Prosecution Decision of the Prosecutor of the Second Special District Court of Jiangsu and Shanghai, Case No. 4 of the 23rd year. Defendant: Li Shu, male, 41 years old, from Xiushan, Sichuan, serving as a secretary in the accounting department of the Third Branch of the Jiangsu High Court, residing at the hospital. The above-mentioned defendant, in the case of suspected dereliction of duty and embezzlement, Case No. 11 of the investigative character in the 33rd year of the Republic of China, has been investigated by this prosecutor, and it is deemed that non-prosecution should be implemented. The facts and reasons are hereby stated as follows: It has been found that the defendant, Li Shu, is a secretary in the accounting department of the Third Branch of the Jiangsu High Court. The plaintiff, Qu Jisheng, and Wang Kang, etc., requested a preliminary injunction due to overdue payments and received a ruling ordering the provision of 12,000 yuan in silver dollars as a guarantee. Twelve long-term financial government bonds of the 17th year of the Republic of China from the Ministry of Finance were prepared, with a face value of

12,000 yuan. On January 20th of this year, the bonds were entrusted to lawyer Jialu, who submitted a petition to this court on the 22nd of the same month for use as security. The dispatch office received and sent the bonds to the civil execution office for verification. On March 2nd, the civil execution office transferred the bonds to Li Shu for safekeeping through the fee collection office of the High Court Branch. Later, Qu Jisheng submitted a statement stating that the case had been settled and requested the revocation of the preliminary injunction and the return of the guaranteed bonds. The civil execution office approved the request on October 1st and issued a retrieval order, instructing Qu to present it for collection. At 3:00 PM that afternoon, Li Shu handed over ten sheets of the aforementioned bonds to Qu Jisheng outside his office. After receiving them, Qu Jisheng went back into the office. Immediately Qu Jisheng shouted, presented the ticket that it was short, entered the room, searched and questioned Li Shu, who replied that he was unaware of the situation and that he should talk to the court. Qu Jisheng said that the bond tickets did not match and did not want to receive them, requesting that the delivery order be returned. Li Shu refused, saying that it had already been registered and canceled, and because Qu Jisheng

was persistently pestering him, he ordered him out. This is based on the records in the case receipt book, civil execution book, payment notification slip, temporary receipt report, the daily fee collection book with the accounting department's seal, the delivery order, the disbursement report, the receipt, and the original petition, as well as the statements of Qu Jisheng, Li Shu, Ren Fugui, etc., which are extremely clear. According to the plaintiff's intention, the interest coupons attached to the original twelve bonds were all due on September 30th of this year. When the due interest coupons were returned, the face value was short of 150 silver dollars. Since the bonds were returned by the defendant and were missing, he is suing them. It should be investigated whether the defendant has clipped the interest coupons or not, as the standard for determining the responsibility for the incident. According to the use of Qu Jisheng, the original each had September 30th of this year,

due interest coupons is true, and according to Bian Jialu, the same is true. However, the original bond tickets were borrowed by Qu Jisheng on January 20th and sent to Bian Jialu. Bian Jialu then submitted the petition to the dispatch office on January 12th, and it was transferred to the defendant on March 2nd. Since the defendant had read it many days later, and since it was handled by people, a careful reading of the documents shows that, apart from the sentence [interest coupon face value from September 30th, Republic of China year 23] in Qu Jisheng's petition on January 22nd, only one entry is found within the original documentary evidence in the case receiving book, the civil execution book, and various receipts which states twelve long-term financial government bonds of the 17th year of the Republic of China with a face value of 12,000 yuan, and there is no mention of interest coupons. After separately summoning the secretaries and clerks of each section in charge of receiving and transferring the bonds for collective questioning, it was stated that the entry of the incoming bond ticket was initially copied into the book based on the documentary evidence column on the incoming petition. That is, the books, delivery forms, and transfers

were based on the records in the incoming documents. No attention was paid to whether interest coupons were attached or not. Therefore, when the bond ticket reached the defendant, it could not be determined whether the interest coupons due on September 30th, as claimed by Qu Jisheng, were still attached. In other words, there is no sufficient positive proof that the interest coupons were actually handed over to the defendant for receipt and safekeeping, and it cannot be hastily concluded that the defendant clipped the interest coupons. Furthermore, inquiries were made with various banks in central China that handled the interest payments and the National Debt Fund Management Committee, and it was determined that the interest coupons had not been paid out. When questioning Qu Jisheng, he was ordered to present the original bond ticket to examine the situation of the clipped interest coupons. He claimed that after retrieving the bond ticket, he had returned it to the original person to sell it. Therefore, it is no longer possible to investigate the truth of how they were clipped. Furthermore, there is no collateral evidence that can be investigated. Since it cannot provide evidence unfavorable to the defendant, a finding favorable to the defendant can be made. It should be considered that there is insufficient suspicion of a crime, and in accordance with Article 244, Section 2 of the Criminal Procedure Law, a decision of non-prosecution is hereby issued. November 24th, 23rd year of the Republic of China, Wang Ren, Prosecutor of the Second Special District Court of Jiangsu and Shanghai.

Incoming: The Crisis of China and the World 149

Dr. Eddy's Speech, Bingxun Stenography Society, Shen Wan Stenography

The well-known American orator, Dr. Eddy, gave his first public speech at Moore Hall, entitled [The Crisis of China and the World], chaired by Dr. Tu Yuqing, translated by Mr. Shen Tilan, and recorded by Shen Wan of the Bingxun Stenography Society. The record of his speech is as follows: This time I traveled around the world, passing through twenty countries, and in China, I passed through twenty large cities. When we left the United States, President Roosevelt was staying in France to save the American economic panic, and wanted to use a new system to remedy this economic panic. Later, when I arrived in the United Kingdom, I also saw the British Prime Minister, also for the sake of economic panic, wanting to save the British economic panic. This kind of global economic panic first occurred in the United States, the United Kingdom, and Germany, and later affected China and the entire world. When I arrived in Germany, I heard Hitler's speech, he told people that in order to implement his ideas, he killed seventy-seven people. If anyone wanted to oppose him, he would treat that person in the same way. However, in Germany, many people are unemployed, and they hope all day long how to overthrow him, because he doesn't give them bread to eat, and he doesn't give them work to do. When I was in Soviet Russia, I also saw that Soviet Russia produced a new system. The people there are not unemployed, but the bread problem is still as serious as ever. Although they have a method of distributing bread, they still cannot solve this problem. We have seen that since the European war, the vitality of the economic situation in various countries around the world has not been fully restored. We see that the whole world is in a state of economic panic. This kind of economic panic indicates that there is a major problem with the modern social system, so we must find a way to save it. Now there is unrest in the whole world, political unrest, students are dissatisfied with the existing system, there is economic panic, and there are many unemployed people everywhere. Students have no jobs. In the United States, one-fourth of the students are unemployed, and they rely on relief to survive. The government is discussing relief methods. Now, many students in China are also unemployed, and they don't know what to do or where to go to find a way out. Why are they unemployed to this extent? The people and workers of all countries in the world are suffering. Looking at it from a historical perspective, I believe that now is a time of transformation, greater than the era of the Renaissance, and greater than the revolutions in the United States, France, and Soviet Russia. Now we have reached a new era of progress, and the old system is collapsing. We know that every historical transformation is accompanied by suffering. Students, workers, and farmers suffer, that is, ordinary people also suffer. We know that mankind, in history, must go through four economic stages. Under the feudal system, we can find that serfs are appendages of landlords. Under the feudal system, landlords have a lot of land, and people and land can be sold in the same way. Under the capitalist system, a small number of people have the means of production, and the majority of people use the means of production of a small number of people to make a living. A small number of people have patents on these means of production, such as tap water, electric lights, kerosene, and various other things, which are all in the hands of a small number of people. A small number of people get too much benefit, and they don't know how to use it. Too many people get too little benefit, and they cannot survive, so there will be turmoil. A small number of people have money, and the majority of people are poor. Under the socialist system, everyone can produce, contribute, and sometimes it may not be easy to have a violent action. In the Danish or British Labor Party, there is no such move. Today, we have reached a stage that is coming to an end. Capitalism is collapsing day by day. In China, the feudal system is collapsing. In the United States, capitalism is also collapsing. This is a period of transformation. Widespread unemployment indicates the selfishness of the past. Therefore, there is a crisis in China, a crisis in the United States, a crisis in Europe, and a crisis in the world. (To be continued)

Education News

National Labor Exhibition, Day Two 150

Extremely Crowded Yesterday, Over Ten Thousand Visitors

Starting Today, Admission by Ticket Required Except for Groups

(Nanjing, 2nd) The 2nd was a Sunday, and people from all walks of life went to visit the National Labor Exhibition in an endless stream. The exhibition venue was small, and there were too many products from various provinces, which were not enough to display. Therefore, the sidewalk in the venue was reduced to less than three feet, and two people could not walk side by side. Initially, it was not expected that there would be more than 10,000 visitors, resulting in a crowded venue, poor order, and exhibits being knocked down. This happened in every hall. In order to remedy the situation, the organizing committee closed the entrance gate at 4:00 PM, allowing people to exit but not enter, and temporarily issued admission tickets. An urgent notice was issued stating that, starting from the 3rd, admission to the exhibition would be by ticket only. In addition to the schedule for primary and secondary schools to visit, admission tickets have been sent to all agencies and universities in the capital. Please ask the leaders of your respective agencies for them. Other sectors of society, please go to the Propaganda Office of the Ministry of Education to collect tickets before coming to the exhibition. Those without tickets will not be admitted. More military police have been dispatched to maintain order. Exhibits in each hall will be reorganized overnight. Visitors such as Ye Chucang and Shao Yuanchong have expressed their opinions on the evaluation book.

Problems Discovered in the Labor Exhibition Wu Yan Yin 152

The labor exhibition, the initial labor exhibition, we naturally should not demand perfection from it. However, from the impression I got after browsing it once, in addition to the positive aspects of being beautiful and having a bit of a creative spirit, there seem to be several problems that can be raised for research in the negative aspects.

(1) There seems to be too little agricultural work in primary and secondary schools.

Our country is an agricultural country, and the social economy has not yet broken away from the agricultural era. Primary and secondary schools, especially primary schools and normal schools, should pay great attention to agricultural work. Because many primary school students are children of farmers, and there are not a few normal school graduates who become rural instructors. Paying attention to agricultural work to enable them to have knowledge and skills in agricultural work, and to have the ideals and attempts to improve agriculture, is very important. The number of achievements in agricultural work in this labor exhibition is very small, which shows that there are too few primary and secondary schools that actually pay attention to agricultural work. This may be because most of the exhibits are from urban primary and secondary schools and children of citizens, but urban primary and secondary schools should also have some achievements in fields such as gardening and animal husbandry.

(2) It seems that handicrafts in primary and secondary schools still focus on delicate small-piece handicrafts.

The exhibits this time are very different from the handicrafts of more than ten years ago, which were just paper-folding and paper-weaving. However, there are still few practical exhibits, and most of them are small models, toys, stationery, etc., which still cannot get rid of the old-fashioned handicraft style. Primary school children can only stick to the slogan of "making toys when they are young, and making airplanes when they grow up," but older primary school students, junior high school students, and normal school students should make more large-scale items such as furniture and school equipment. Because the most important goal of labor education is to cultivate the ability of children and young people to work, and to make them sweat more. If we focus solely on delicate small-piece handicrafts, it is still almost the same as the old-fashioned scholar's seal engraving, painting, and calligraphy. At best, it is just using the hands. If the body does not labor, where will the sweat come from?

(3) It seems that the various exhibits of primary and secondary schools focus more on aestheticization and less on the meaning of production.

Although there are many practical and popular exhibits, such as local agricultural household appliances, most of the achievements still seem to be working on the aesthetic side, and the meaning of production is very small. Beauty is an important condition for crafts, sewing, etc., but if you pursue beauty too much, one is that it wastes a lot of effort and energy for children and young people, and it may not conform to the principles of economics, and the other is that it is often delicate but not practical, and the production value will not be seen much. In the exhibition, people compete for novelty and uniqueness, fearing that the exhibits are not beautiful, in order to win the admiration of the audience. This is the common psychology of people, but labor work is labor's work, and labor is the work of labor, the most important thing is not to lose the meaning of production education, and it is very different from fine arts and artworks. If you deliberately seek workmanship, regardless of labor costs, and it is not necessarily possible to sell it.

(4) The exhibits from a small number of places seem to be inevitably miscellaneous.

The exhibits from most places are generally still between labor work and handicraft, and they also have their own characteristics. Some of the imitation instruments are no different from commodities, and more teaching aids have the meaning of creativity and invention. However, some places not only have very few exhibits, but also inevitably have miscellaneous items. For example, the collected plant specimens, and the fabric samples collected by primary school students, etc., although made by students, are not achievements within the scope of the labor course. Also, paintings and sculptures, etc., from non-art schools are actually treated as labor achievements and transported here as an example, which is even beyond the scope of labor work. The staff in charge of labor work thought that if they removed these kinds of things, the labor exhibits from some provinces would be even less, so they still let them be displayed, but it is too far from the meaning of the labor exhibition.

The above four points are the main points I have noticed. In addition, some exhibits take foreign raw materials at will, some exhibits are made in foreign styles, and some exhibits seem to exceed the production capacity of students, which inevitably makes people doubt... These are all small details, and I won't say much. I think this is a phenomenon that should exist in the initial exhibits. I hope that primary and secondary schools will pay attention to improving labor education and make extra efforts in the future. According to my opinion, the aspects of future efforts are:

(1) Primary and secondary schools and normal schools should pay attention to agricultural work, and at least have some facilities such as gardening.

(2) If primary and secondary schools and normal schools focus on crafts, the equipment of the factory must be complete, so that students can do more large-scale labor practice. (3) Primary and secondary schools and normal schools should pay attention to cultivating labor teachers at all levels in order to improve labor education.

(4) Primary and secondary schools and normal schools should implement the labor curriculum standards in a practical way, and not continue to follow the old-fashioned handicraft practices.

(5) The principle of labor work exhibits in middle schools should be production, and although primary school labor works cannot be directly produced, they also have some educational significance of production.

As for the exhibits of vocational schools, they are naturally more neat than the exhibits of primary and secondary schools. However, in China, which emphasizes agriculture, there are too few agricultural vocational schools, so the achievements of agricultural schools in this labor exhibition are not easy to attract attention. How to promote the establishment of more agricultural vocational schools in the future is something that educational administrators should pay close attention to.

Exiting the third hall and going down the stairs, Achievement Hall is the location of the fourth hall. Entering a small room is the exhibition area for the experimental school of the Central University. Turning into the fourth hall, it is full of brilliance, as if entering a large art museum. What is displayed is

Hunan's Hunan embroidery. There are 150 items of this embroidery on display, most of which are framed calligraphy and paintings. There are also seven embroidered portraits on the walls, which are portraits of Sun Yat-sen, Chairman Lin, Chairman Chiang, He Jian, and others. They are exquisitely made and breathtaking. There are about 100 items of sewing, most of which are packed in paper boxes. In addition, there are more than 80 mechanical items, 200 items of dyeing and weaving, about 120 items of applied chemistry, about 20 items of agricultural products, about 15 items of silk, and about 1,000 items of other labor works such as metalwork, woodwork, and carving. Many of them are exquisite and elegant.

Shanghai City Exhibits (Photo by Zhonghua, Nanjing)

Hubei occupies the central part of the fourth hall. There are about 1,000 exhibits in total. There is a rockery garden in the middle, and there are many machine-woven fabrics, metalwork, woodwork, and chemical crafts. The representative of the province, Mr. Ma, is arranging everything by himself, and he is very busy. The wooden warship models, rattan characters, and wooden couplets are all very exquisite. Turning from here to

The four most outstanding items are: (1) Lacquerware produced by the Huier Institute, such as vases, figure screens, plates, boxes, cups, etc., all of which are very exquisite. The school is a work-study program, so students pay great attention to hand-brain training. The sale of lacquerware in Fujian has occupied an important position. The exhibits participating in the exhibition this time are worth about 4,000 to 5,000 yuan. (2) The projection and architectural specimens of the Provincial Industrial Vocational School. These specimens are accurately manufactured and are the most important instruments of the industrial school. It is said that if purchased from abroad, each set costs about 1,000 yuan or more. Now the school can make it by itself at a low price, only one-tenth of the imported products. (3) Rattanware. Fujian has a long history of making rattanware, and the rattanware products are far better than those of other provinces. (4) Bamboo ware, including a complete set of structures for study rooms and living rooms, etc., is very good. The method of display is also in accordance with the standards of each hall. Crafts, agricultural products, manufactured goods, balances, and other metalwork items are all items actually sold on the market. The silk products of the girls' school are very modern. The venue has come to an end. The reporter then exited the venue. There are 26 participating units, with about 30,000 exhibits. To sum up this tour, although it only lasted a few hours, the impressions gained were excellent and profound. It is lamentable that our country has always regarded scholars as the head of the four classes of people, those who labor with their minds rule others, and those who labor with their strength are ruled by others. Therefore, the whole country is filled with the idea of ​​"study well and then become an official". The so-called "strange skills and lascivious ingenuity" are called "mean husbands", so the industry is backward, and those who know it regard it as a hidden worry. In recent years, the central education authorities have vigorously promoted production education, and education experts from all over the country have been able to embrace the spirit of poverty and hard work, and work together to achieve this great achievement. This is what we should express our admiration for. Secondly, the products of vocational schools and the labor works of primary and secondary schools are gradually becoming more practical, unlike in the past, when they were merely decorations, in order to win the appreciation of a few artists, and various self-made teaching aids and design units can fully express the progress of today's teaching. This is especially admirable. Since the September 18th Incident, the people of the whole country have a psychology of common hatred for the enemy. The weapons that occupy a large part of the exhibits in various provinces show that colleagues in the education sector pay attention to national defense education. It is deeply hoped that all sectors of society in the country will pay special attention to this conference, in order to correct the past errors of education for officials, then this conference, although it costs the efforts of tens of thousands of people, will have an immortal value.
